Rugrats Core Intrinsic API¶

Introduction¶

This chapter introduces the intrinsics for RiVAI Rugrats core programming, including type system, csr configure operations and vector operations.

Type System¶

Instruction

Results

rd -> result

csrr rd,vxrm

rd -> result

csrr rd,vtype

rd -> result

csrr rd,vxsat

rd -> result

rd -> result

csrr rd,vmgroupdepth

rd -> result

rd -> result

CSR Scalar Write Intrinsic function list¶

Intrinsic

Arguments

Instruction

void vwr_csr(RUGRATS_VXRM, int value)

value -> rs1

csrw vxrm,rs1

void vwr_csr(RUGRATS_VMELEMENTSTRIDE, int value)

value -> rs1

csrw vmelementstride,rs1

void vwr_csr(RUGRATS_VMGROUPDEPTH, int value)

value -> rs1

csrw vmgroupdepth,rs1

void vwr_csr(RUGRATS_VMGROUPSTRIDE, int value)

value -> rs1

csrw vmgroupstride,rs1

void vwr_csr(RUGRATS_VMGROUPNUMBER, int value)

value -> rs1

csrw vmgroupnumber,rs1

void vwr_csr(RUGRATS_VMCOMBOSTRIDE, int value)

value -> rs1

csrw vmcombostride,rs1

void vwr_csr(RUGRATS_VIIR, int value)

value -> rs1

csrw viir,rs1

CSR immediate Write Intrinsic function list¶

Intrinsic

Arguments

Instruction

void vwr_csri(RUGRATS_VXRM, int8_t imm)

0 <= imm < 4

csrwi vxrm,#imm

void vwr_csri(RUGRATS_VMELEMENTSTRIDE, int8_t imm)

-16 <= imm <= 15

csrwi vmelementstride,#imm

void vwr_csri(RUGRATS_VMGROUPDEPTH, int8_t imm)

-16 <= imm <= 15

csrwi vmgroupdepth,#imm

void vwr_csri(RUGRATS_VMGROUPSTRIDE, int8_t imm)

-16 <= imm <= 15

csrwi vmgroupstride,#imm

void vwr_csri(RUGRATS_VMGROUPNUMBER, int8_t imm)

-16 <= imm <= 15

csrwi vmgroupnumber,#imm

void vwr_csri(RUGRATS_VMCOMBOSTRIDE, int8_t imm)

-16 <= imm <= 15

csrwi vmcombostride,#imm

void vwr_csri(RUGRATS_VIIR, int8_t imm)

0 <= imm <= 31

csrwi viir,#imm
